<li data-start="465" data-end="516">
<p data-start="468" data-end="516">Keep it <strong data-start="476" data-end="486">Public</strong> and check “Add a README file”</p>
</li>
<li data-start="517" data-end="547">
<p data-start="520" data-end="547">Click <strong data-start="526" data-end="547">Create repository</strong></p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="549" data-end="552">
<h4 data-start="554" data-end="589">✅ Step 2: Upload Website Files</h4>
<ol data-start="590" data-end="809">
<li data-start="590" data-end="630">
<p data-start="593" data-end="630">Click <strong data-start="599" data-end="630">“Add file” → “Upload files”</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="631" data-end="731">
<p data-start="634" data-end="731">Copy the full HTML code I gave you (or download <span class="" data-state="closed"><a data-start="682" data-end="730" class="cursor-pointer">this file</a></span>)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="732" data-end="781">
<p data-start="735" data-end="781">Upload the file and rename it to: <code data-start="769" data-end="781">index.html</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="782" data-end="809">
<p data-start="785" data-end="809">Click <strong data-start="791" data-end="809">Commit changes</strong></p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="811" data-end="814">
<h4 data-start="816" data-end="850">✅ Step 3: Enable GitHub Pages</h4>
<ol data-start="851" data-end="983">
<li data-start="851" data-end="897">
<p data-start="854" data-end="897">Go to your repository: <strong data-start="877" data-end="897">Settings → Pages</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="898" data-end="965">
<p data-start="901" data-end="965">Under <strong data-start="907" data-end="919">“Source”</strong>, choose <strong data-start="928" data-end="944">Branch: main</strong> and <strong data-start="949" data-end="965">folder: root</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="966" data-end="983">
<p data-start="969" data-end="983">Click <strong data-start="975" data-end="983">Save</strong></p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="985" data-end="1044">After a few seconds, GitHub will give you a live link like:</p>
<blockquote data-start="1046" data-end="1097">
<p data-start="1048" data-end="1097">🌐 <code data-start="1051" data-end="1097">https://yourusername.github.io/postal-mitra/</code></p>
</blockquote>
<hr data-start="1099" data-end="1102">
<h3 data-start="1104" data-end="1123">🚀 You're Live!</h3>
<p data-start="1124" data-end="1223">Share that link with your customers. The form will redirect to your WhatsApp for every application.</p>
